create or replace PROCEDURE BRF207_DETAIL_PROCEDURE (REPORT_DATE DATE)
IS
  V_REPORT_DATE DATE := To_date (REPORT_DATE, 'DD-MM-YYYY'); 
   V_FROM_DATE dATE :=  ADD_MONTHS (LAST_DAY (REPORT_DATE), -1) + 1;
BEGIN

delete from BRF207_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE;
Commit;

INSERT INTO BRF207_DETAILTABLE
(
    foracid,
    cust_id,
    ACCT_NAME,
    REPORT_DATE,
    REPORT_LABEL_1,
    REPORT_NAME_1,
    report_addl_criteria_1
)

SELECT
    foracid,
    cust_id,
    ACCT_NAME,
    REPORT_DATE,
    REPORT_LABEL_1,
    REPORT_NAME_1,
    report_addl_criteria_1
FROM
   BRF207_MAPPING_TABLE
WHERE
    REPORT_DATE = TO_DATE('30-JUN-2023', 'DD-MON-YYYY')
    AND REPORT_LABEL_1 IS NOT NULL;

MERGE INTO BRF207_DETAILTABLE A
USING ( SELECT ACCT_NUMBER, ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC FROM GENERAL_MASTER_TABLE) B
ON (A.foracid = B.ACCT_NUMBER)
WHEN MATCHED THEN
  UPDATE SET A.ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC = B.ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC;
  COMMIT;
  
  DELETE FROM BRF207_DETAILTABLE WHERE REPORT_NAME_1 IS NULL;
COMMIT;




COMMIT;
END;

create or replace PROCEDURE  "BRF207_MAPPING_PROCEDURE" ( REPORT_DATE VARCHAR2) 
IS 

  V_REPORT_DATE DATE := To_date (REPORT_DATE, 'DD-MM-YYYY');

--NBFI
insert into BRF207_mapping_table
( foracid, cust_id, ACCT_NAME,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,GL_CODE,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,SOL_ID,SCHM_CODE,CONSTITUTION_CODE,COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,COUNTRY)
SELECT  ACCT_NUMBER,cust_id, ACCT_NAME,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,GL_CODE,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,SOL_ID,SCHM_CODE,CONSTITUTION_CODE,COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,COUNTRY
FROM GENERAL_MASTER_TABLE  where report_date = v_report_date 
and SCHM_CODE IN  ( 'CA101', 'CA102', 'CA103', 'CA106','CA107',
'CA108', 'CA109', 'CA110', 'CA111', 'CA112', 'LA101', 'LA106', 'OD001', 'OD002', 'OD003', 'OD028', 'OD651', 'SB105', 'SB207',
'TD115','SB101', 'SB102', 'SB103', 'SB106', 'SB110', 'SB201',
'SB203', 'SB303', 'TD101', 'TD102', 'TD103', 'TD105', 'TD106', 'TD108', 'TD109','TD112', 'TD301') ;
commit;

IS
---VARIABLE DECLARE
V_REPORT_DATE DATE := TO_DATE(Report_date,'DD-MM-YYYY');
V_REPORT_FROM_DATE DATE := Add_Months( Last_day (V_REPORT_DATE), -6)+1;
V_REPORT_TO_DATE DATE := V_REPORT_DATE;

---DECLARATION
V_R1_PRODUCT VARCHAR2(150 BYTE):='CASH BALANCES WITH CENTRAL BANK';
